add_namespace = MD4_election
add_namespace = western_win
add_namespace = emerging_win
add_namespace = salafist_win
add_namespace = non_alligned_win
add_namespace = nationalist_win
add_namespace = MD4_election_campaign
add_namespace = News_MD4_election
add_namespace = coalition
add_namespace = coalition_complete
add_namespace = coalition_pass

#### finished forming ###
news_event = {
	id = coalition_complete.0
	title = coalition_complete.0.t
	desc = coalition_complete.0.d
	picture = GFX_news_press_conference
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = coalition_complete.0.a #add to coalition
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: coalition_complete.0.a executed"
		
		add_political_power = 25
		
	}
}


#### Pass to new party to form coalition ###
country_event = {
	id = coalition_pass.0
	title = coalition_pass.0.t
	desc = coalition_pass.0.d
	picture = GFX_news_press_conference
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
	#some find biggest in array function
		
	}
	
	#options to pass to one of 2 biggest parties, only 1 if you are one of them.
	#pass to biggest
	option = {
		name = coalition_pass.0.a 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: coalition_pass.0.a executed"
		
		hidden_effect = {
				refund_government_coalition = yes #give 75% of invested PP back
				clear_array = gov_coalition_array
				clear_array = ruling_party
		}
		add_political_power = -150
	}
	#pass to second biggest
	option = {
		name = coalition_pass.0.b 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: coalition_pass.0.b executed"
		
		hidden_effect = {
				refund_government_coalition = yes #give 75% of invested PP back
				clear_array = gov_coalition_array
				clear_array = ruling_party
		}
		add_political_power = -150
	}
	#Stick with current, go back
	option = {
		name = coalition_pass.0.c 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: coalition_pass.0.c executed"
	}
}



#### invite conservatism event ####

#Western_Autocracy - 0
country_event = {
	id = coalition.0
	title = coalition.0.t
	desc = coalition.0.d
	picture = GFX_politics_speak
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = coalition.0.a #add to coalition
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = coalition_formed } }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: coalition.0.a executed"
		
		add_political_power = pp_cost_to_invite
		add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 }
		update_government_coalition_strength = yes
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
			}
			clear_coalition_western_count_ideas = yes
			reset_democratic_coalition_ideas = yes
		}
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { government_coalition_strength_elect > majority_threshold } } 
			set_country_flag = coalition_formed
			ROOT = { news_event = { id = coalition_complete.0 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = coalition.0.b #
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: coalition.0.b executed"
		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { coalition_democratic = party_pop_elect_array^0 }
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_politics_left_wing
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		
	}

		name = coalition.10.a #add to coalition
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = coalition_formed } }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: coalition.10.a executed"
		
		add_political_power = pp_cost_to_invite
		add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 10 }
		update_government_coalition_strength = yes
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}
			clear_coalition_salafist_count_ideas = yes
			reset_fascism_coalition_ideas = yes
		}
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { government_coalition_strength_elect > majority_threshold } } 
			set_country_flag = coalition_formed
			ROOT = { news_event = { id = coalition_complete.0 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = coalition.10.b #
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: coalition.10.b executed"
		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { coalition_fascism = party_pop_elect_array^10 }
		}
	}
}

			ROOT = { news_event = { id = coalition_complete.0 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = coalition.15.b #
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: coalition.15.b executed"
		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { coalition_neutrality = party_pop_elect_array^15 }
		}
	}
}

### Initial event, launches everything else
country_event = {
	id = MD4_election_campaign.0
	title = MD4_election_campaign.0.t
	desc = MD4_election_campaign.0.d
	picture = GFX_election_day
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		display_election_campaign_status = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = MD4_election_campaign.0.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: MD4_election_campaign.0.a executed"
		campaign_spending_effects = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = MD4_election_campaign.80 days = 14 } #Final results
			country_event = { id = MD4_election_campaign.1 days = 1 } #choose what you want to do
		}
	}
}

#Choose If they want to promote a party/outlooks or attack it
country_event = {
	id = MD4_election_campaign.1
	title = MD4_election_campaign.1.t
	desc = MD4_election_campaign.1.d
	picture = GFX_election_day
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#choose to attack
	option = {
		name = MD4_election_campaign.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: MD4_election_campaign.1.a executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = MD4_election_campaign.2 }
		}
	}
	
	#Choose to support
	option = {
		name = MD4_election_campaign.1.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: MD4_election_campaign.1.a executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = MD4_election_campaign.41 }
		}
	}
}

#Attack Western
country_event = {
	id = MD4_election_campaign.3
	title = MD4_election_campaign.3.t
	desc = MD4_election_campaign.3.d
	picture = GFX_election_day
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Outlook as a whole
	option = {
		name = MD4_election_campaign.3.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: MD4_election_campaign.3.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 1
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 5
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_2 = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = -0.01 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 4
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 8
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_4 = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = -0.02 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 7
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 11
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_8 = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = -0.04 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 10
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 15
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_12 = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = -0.06 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 14
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 17
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_16 = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = -0.08 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		
		#If the negative campaign backfires
		random_list = {
			80 = { }
			20 = { country_event = { id = MD4_election_campaign.4 days = 8 } }
		}
	}
	
	#Conservative
	option = {
		name = MD4_election_campaign.3.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: MD4_election_campaign.3.b executed"

			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 1
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 5
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_2 = yes
			add_to_variable = { conservatism_pop = -0.01 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 4
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 8
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_4 = yes
			add_to_variable = { conservatism_pop = -0.02 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 7
					}
					has_country_flag = {

				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_8 = yes

	desc = MD4_election_campaign.4.d
	picture = GFX_election_rally

	immediate = {
	}
	
	option = {
		name = MD4_election_campaign.4.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: MD4_election_campaign.4.a executed"	
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 1
					}

						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 5
					}
				}
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.02 }
			recalculate_party = yes
			relative_change_neg_4 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {

					}
					has_country_flag = {

					}
				}
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.04 }

			relative_change_neg_4 = yes

						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 7

					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 11
					}
				}
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.08 }
			recalculate_party = yes
			relative_change_neg_4 = yes

	title = MD4_election_campaign.16.t
	desc = MD4_election_campaign.16.d
	picture = GFX_election_rally
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
	}
	
	option = {
		name = MD4_election_campaign.16.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: MD4_election_campaign.16.a executed"	
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 1
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 5
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { Vilayat_e_Faqih_pop = 0.02 }
			recalculate_party = yes
			relative_change_neg_4 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 4
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 8
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { Vilayat_e_Faqih_pop = 0.04 }
			recalculate_party = yes
			relative_change_neg_4 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 7
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 11
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { Vilayat_e_Faqih_pop = 0.08 }
			recalculate_party = yes
			relative_change_neg_4 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 10
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 15
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { Vilayat_e_Faqih_pop = 0.12 }
			recalculate_party = yes
			relative_change_neg_4 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 14
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 17
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { Vilayat_e_Faqih_pop = 0.16 }
			recalculate_party = yes
			relative_change_neg_4 = yes
		}
	}
}

#Attack Salafist
country_event = {
	id = MD4_election_campaign.19
	title = MD4_election_campaign.19.t
	desc = MD4_election_campaign.19.d
	picture = GFX_election_day
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Outlook as a whole
	option = {
		name = MD4_election_campaign.19.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: MD4_election_campaign.19.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 1
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 5
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_2 = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = -0.01 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 4
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 8
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_4 = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = -0.02 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 7
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 11
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_8 = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = -0.04 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 10
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 15
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_12 = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = -0.06 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 14
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 17
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_16 = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = -0.08 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		
		#If the negative campaign backfires
		random_list = {
			80 = { }
			20 = { country_event = { id = MD4_election_campaign.20 days = 8 } }
		}
	}
	
	#Salafist Jihadism
	option = {
		name = MD4_election_campaign.19.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: MD4_election_campaign.19.b executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 1
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 5
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_2 = yes
			add_to_variable = { Kingdom_pop = -0.01 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 4
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 8
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_4 = yes
			add_to_variable = { Kingdom_pop = -0.02 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 7
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 11
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_8 = yes
			add_to_variable = { Kingdom_pop = -0.04 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 10
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 15
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_12 = yes
			add_to_variable = { Kingdom_pop = -0.06 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 14
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count

				}
			}

						value > 7

					has_country_flag = {

					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_8 = yes

			recalculate_party = yes

					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 10
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 15
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_12 = yes
			add_to_variable = { Neutral_Muslim_Brotherhood_pop = -0.06 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 14
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 17
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_16 = yes
			add_to_variable = { Neutral_Muslim_Brotherhood_pop = -0.08 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		
		#If the negative campaign backfires
		random_list = {
			80 = { }
			20 = { country_event = { id = MD4_election_campaign.34 days = 8 } }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = MD4_election_campaign.24.e
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: MD4_election_campaign.25.e executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = MD4_election_campaign.23 }
		}
	}
}

						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value > 14
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = campaign_funding_count
						value < 17
					}
				}
			}
			relative_change_pos_16 = yes
			add_to_variable = { Mod_Vilayat_e_Faqih_pop = 0.08 }
			recalculate_party = yes
		}
		
		#If the negative campaign backfires
		random_list = {
			80 = { }
			20 = { country_event = { id = MD4_election_campaign.56 days = 8 } }
		}
	}
	
	#Even more Emerging Options
	option = {
		name = MD4_election_campaign.49.e
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: MD4_election_campaign.49.e executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = MD4_election_campaign.50 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = western_win.0
	title = western_win.0.t
	desc = western_win.0.d
	picture = GFX_election_day
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		
	}
		
	option = {
		name = western_win.0.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: western_win.0.a executed"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { has_government = democratic }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = MD4_election_campaign.81 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = western_win.0.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: western_win.0.b executed"
		ai_chance = { factor = 80 }
		trigger = { NOT = { has_government = democratic } }
		retire_country_leader = yes
		set_country_flag = { flag = approval_rating value = 50 }
		reset_all_internal_faction_opinions = yes
		set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
				}
		country_event = { id = MD4_election_campaign.81 }
	}
	option = {
		name = western_win.0.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: western_win.0.c executed"
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		trigger = { NOT = { has_government = democratic } }
		increase_corruption = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		recalculate_party = yes
		country_event = { id = MD4_election_campaign.81 }
	}
}
